This way, if you go from point A to point B, you can record the route.\r\n\r\n3) Follow me and don't draw route on the map. In the menu you must click on \"Start follow me / Stop follow me\". This feature is enabled when the option \"Enable track route on map\" in the settings menu is not checked.
